# CX Knowledgebase : CRM/Agent Desk Post Message Events

The Expertflow CX sends following events to CRM via JavaScript post messages when CRM integration is enabled in agent desk settings.  


| **USE CASE**| **AGENT DESK EVENTS**| **Intended Attributes**| **QUESTIONS**  
---|---|---|---|---  
1|  When agent state changes| 

##### **Agent presence event**
[code]

| 

##### **State**
[code] 
    "state": { 
       "name": "READY", 
       "reasonCode": null }
[/code]

**possible states :**

  * READY 
  * NOT_READY
  * LOGOUT
  * LOGIN

| Diference between objects ofAgent state change and Mrd state change?  
If the value of this attribue "agentStateChanged" is true,Then Agent state changed,if false then Mrd state is changed.   
2| When MRD state changes|

##### **State**
[code] 
    "state": { 
    "name": "READY",
    "reasonCode": null }
[/code]

**possible states :**

  * READY 
  * NOT_READY
  * BUSY
  * ACTIVE
  * PENDING_NOT_READY

| 

  * Different Agent and MRD State Change? (yes)

  
3| When the agent logged in agent desk| 

##### **Agent Login**
[code] 
    eventName: "AGENT_LOGIN",
    agentData: {
        "id": "4c2659f2-04b8-4a3b-9e7c-c889681689d0",
        "firstName": "",
        "agentData": {
            "id": "4c2659f2-04b8-4a3b-9e7c-c889681689d0",
            "firstName": "",
            "lastName": "",
            "username": "sana",
            "permittedResources": {
                "Resources": [
                    {
                        "scopes": [
                            "view",

| 

##### **State**
[code] 
    "state": { 
    "name": "WRAP_UP", 
    "reasonCode": null 
    }
[/code]

| 

  * Any Specific attribute required in payload? (No , just Complete Payload)

  
9| When the agent ends the conversation| 

##### **End Conversation**
[code] 
     event: "END_CONVERSATION",
     agentData:{
        "agentData": {
            "task": "topicUnsubscription",
            "reason": "UNSUBSCRIBED",
            "conversationId": "65a923832d53786eb16039f0",
            "roomInfo": {
                "id": "65a6027c0e01d858eb846b27",
                "mode": "CONTACT_CENTER"
            },
            "statusCode": 200
        }
    }               
[/code]

| |

| | 

  * Is Conversation Id or Customer Id required in payload?  
(will send both ids)

  
  
External CRM/Systems can send the following commands to EFCX to change the agent/MRD state. In response to these commands, the system will send the [agentPresence event](https://expertflow-docs.atlassian.net/wiki/x/DYVg).

| **USE CASE**| **Commands**| **QUESTIONS**  
---|---|---|---  
1| To change Agent State| 

##### **change agent state**
[code] 
    {
        event:"Connector_Action",
        agentData:{
            action:"agentStateChange",
            agentId:"<id>",
            state: { name: "<state>", reasonCode: null }
    
    }
    
    
    
[/code]

| **Required Data From CRM:**  


  * Required action i.e agentStateChange
  * Agent ID
  * Intended Agent State

  
2| To change MRD State| 

##### **change MRD**
[code] 
    {
        event:"Connector_Action",
        agentData:{
            action:"mrdStateChange",
            mrdId:"<mrd-id>"
            agentId:"<id>",
            state: { name: "<state>", reasonCode: null }
    
    }
[/code]

| **Required Data From CRM:**  


  * Required action i.e mrdStateChange
  * MRD ID
  * Agent ID
  * Intended MRD State

  
  
| **Use Case**| **Task State for Voice Call**| **Input required**  
---|---|---|---  
1| When Voice Call ends|
